Carrying our luggage to the room ourselves was an inconvenience that could have easily been avoided with proper staffing and organization.

It seemed that there were inefficiencies in the hotel's check-in procedures, resulting in unnecessary delays and inconvenience for guests.

posted:Posted January 5, 2024
msg:Close to the airport, but not fully walkable. A taxi is probably still preferred to get to. I believe if you contact the hotel in advance to ask you can find out more about getting a shuttle - it's somewhat easier to go to the airport from the hotel than going from the airport to the hotel.

This is the somewhat 'budget' version of the other Fliport hotels. Hotel rooms are clean enough, with a decent buffet breakfast. There is a pool, gym and very small kids play area. 

Staff are friendly; somewhat minimal English spoken (if that is a concern).

More of a stopover hotel to be near the hotel than a hotel to properly stay and enjoy at.
